		232) <a href="/cgi-bin/app/winslow_query.py?qs=ஞானம்&searchhws=yes&matchtype=exact">ஞானம்</a> ñāṉam
		from <a href="/dictionaries/winslow/">Winslow's <i>"A comprehensive Tamil and English dictionary"</i></a>
		(<a href="/cgi-bin/app/winslow_query.py?page=533">p. 533</a>)
		<blockquote><p>*<hw><tam>ஞானம்</tam></hw> , <i>s.</i> W. p. 355. <smallcaps>GNANA.</smallcaps> Intellect, intelligence, spiritually, <tam>அறிவு</tam>. 2. Knowledge, wisdom, erudition, learning, <tam>கல்வி</tam>. 3. Mystic or recondite knowledge; knowledge of the nature of deity, the soul, intellect, &c., derived from meditation, the teaching of the Guru, experience, self-mortification, &c., and connected with corresponding practice according to the stage of the religionist, <tam>பிரமஞானம்</tam>. 4. The fourth degree in the Saiva system, that of the exalted ascetie who by austerities, is said to have annihilated his passions; freed his soul from earthly desires; and become ripe for absorption, <tam>ஞானபாதம்</tam>. 5. The conduct of the <tam>ஞானி</tam>, or professor of the fourth degree of the Saiva system, <tam>ஞானநடை</tam>. 6. Right knowledge, true wisdom, <tam>மெய்ஞ்ஞானம்</tam>. 7. A spiritual principle, state, quality or stage of the soul, when by the exhaustion of the good and evil influence of former births, it dominates over the immerging principle, ceases from actions, and approaches assimilation to the deity, <tam>தெளிவு</tam>.–This is applicable alike to human and to super- human beings, and to the forms of deity as high as <tam>சதாசிவம்</tam>.–<i>Note.</i> Knowledge in considered attainable in three ways: 1. By evidence of the senses, perception, &c. 2. Inference. 3. Divine revelation. These are subdivided into sixty-five varieties. <tam>ஞானம்</tam>, is two-fold: 1. <tam>விடையஞானம்</tam>, worldly or secular knowledge. 2. <tam>சொரூபஞானம்</tam>, divine or spiritual knowledge of the nature of deity, spirit and <tam>பாசம்</tam>, with a state of soul approximating toward union with the universal spirit. <p2><tam>ஞானகஞ்சுகன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The deity as pure intelligence clothed with wisdom. <i>(p.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>ஞானகாண்டம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Those parts of the Vedas which inculcate mystic and spiritual knowledge, abstract devotion, &c. See <tam>கிரியாகாண்டம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானகாண்டிகர்</tam>, <i>s. (plu.)</i> Those who have obtained the spiritual knowledge, and who practise the abstract devotion inculcated in the <tam>ஞானகாண்டம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானகாரணி</tam>, <i>s.</i> The authoress of wisdom.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானகாரியம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual matters, things connected with the essentials of religion.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானகுரு</tam>–<tam>ஞானசாரியன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The spiritual guru; <i>i. e.</i> the deity appearing in human form, for the instruction and illumination of his disciples; or the deity represented by the officiating guru.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானக்கண்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual sight, vision, illumination–oppos. to <tam>ஊனக்கண்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானக்களை</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual luster, in the countenance of an advanced devotee.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானக்காட்சி</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual perception. 2. Spiritual sight or vision of the <tam>ஞானி</tam>, Who professes to view at once all things in the universe.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசத்தி</tam>, <i>s.</i> One of the six <tam>சத்தி</tam> or female energies of deity.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசபை</tam>, <i>s.</i> A hall at <tam>சிதம்பரம்</tam>, symbolizing the immensity of God, without an idol, and intended to represent the visible heavens. see <tam>சிற்சபை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசமாதி</tam>, <i>s.</i> The posture of the erect silent ascetic of the highest degree, superior to the Yogi. See <tam>சமாதி</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசரிதர்</tam>, <i>s. (plu.)</i> Those who practice the rules of the fourth degree.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசரீரம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The spiritual body.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசாதனம்</tam>–<tam>ஞானசாதனை</tam>, <i>s.</i> Practice in the devotions of the <tam>ஞானி</tam> before he has arrived at the fourth or highest stage. See <tam>ஞானம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசாத்திரம்</tam>–<tam>ஞானநூல்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Theology, or the science which treats of the nature of the supreme Being, the soul and other mysteries of religion. This is two-fold: 1. <tam>பூர்வம்</tam>. 2. <tam>சித்தாந்தம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசிகாமணி</tam>, <i>s.</i> God, as crowning all wisdom.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசுகம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The highest enjoyments, those of the advanced devotee, who by abstractions has deified himself and become fit for absorption.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசூட்சம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Occult meaning, spiritual interpretation. 2. A clue to the understanding of the mystical parts of religion.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானசூரியன்</tam>, <i>s. (christ. usage.)</i> The sun of Righteousness, Jesus christ.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானச்சுடர்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The deity as the possessor of spiritual light.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானதிசை</tam>–<tam>ஞானதசை</tam>, <i>s.</i> The state, or the season, when a soul is ripening for emancipation; or when secular influences cease and spiritual motives operate. See <tam>பெத்ததிசை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானதிடம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> True wisdom. See <tam>மெய்ஞ்ஞானம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானதிட்டி</tam>–<tam>ஞானதிருஷ்டி</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual light or illumination, said to be attained by exalted devotees. 2. The official look of the guru, on the advanced disciple, in the administration of the <tam>சிவதீட்சை</tam>, supposed to dispel sin (<tam>மலம்</tam>) and impart illumination, &c. <tam>ஞானதிருட்டியைவிழித்தல்</tam>. Opening the eyes of the mind, or awakening spiritual sight, as a guru for the benefit of his disciple.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானதீட்சை</tam>, <i>s.</i> The imparting of spiritual illumination, by the look of the guru in his official capacity, or fancied visible personification of the deity, by which the <tam>சஞ்சிதம்</tam> or former evils of the mature disciple are consumed and he is advanced toward heaven. Compare <tam>குருதீட்சை</tam>. 2. <i>(R. C. usage.)</i> The rite of baptism.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானதீபம்</tam>-<tam>ஞானதீபிகை</tam>-<tam>ஞானவிளக்கு</tam>, <i>s.</i> The lamp of knowledge.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானத்தகப்பன்</tam>, <i>s. (Christ. usage.)</i> A sponsor to a child in baptism; a god- father.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானத்தாய்</tam>, <i>s. (Christ. usage.)</i> A god- mother.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானஸ்நானம்</tam>, <i>s. (Christ. usage.)</i> Baptism. See <tam>ஸ்நானம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானஸ்நானங்கொடுக்க</tam>–<tam>ஞானஸ்நானம் பண்ண</tam>, <i>inf.</i> to baptize.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானஸ்நானம்பெற</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To receive baptism.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானநாயகன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The Supreme Being as the author and object of <tam>ஞானம்</tam> to the devotee, or lord of spiritual illumination, <tam>கடவுள்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானநிட்டை</tam>–<tam>ஞானநிஷ்டை</tam>, <i>s.</i> The devotion of the <tam>ஞானி</tam>, as a silent worshipper, having the mind fixed on a divine object, &c.; a higher stage than <tam>ஞானசாதனை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானநிலை</tam>, <i>s.</i> The fourth degree in the Saiva system, that of the <tam>ஞானி</tam> or the practisers of that degree. 2. Eastablishment in that degree.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானநிறைவு</tam>–<tam>ஞானபூர்த்தி</tam>, <i>s.</i> Perfect knowledge.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானநூல்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Theological treatises, &c. See <tam>ஞானசாத்திரம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபைத்தியம்</tam>–<tam>ஞானப்பயித்தியம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Apparent aberration of mind caused by divine abstractions, contemplations, &c. 2. Religious melancholy.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபரன்</tam>–<tam>ஞானகுருபரன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> God, the deity in human form, as spiritual teacher and illuminator of the advanced disciple. See <tam>ஞானகுரு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபாகை</tam>, <i>s.</i> One of the three parts of the Vedas, that which relates to spiritual, mystic matters. See <tam>பாகை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபாதம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The fourth or highest degree in the Saiva system–as <tam>ஞானநிலை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபாரகன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> One well versed in the fourth degree.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபுத்திரன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A spiritual son or disciple.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபூசை</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual worship, or worship appropriate to the fourth or highest degree.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபூர்த்தி</tam>, <i>s.</i> As <tam>ஞானநிறைவு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபூர்வகம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Prescience, foreknowledge.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானப்பால்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A section of a book treating of divine knowledge. 2. <i>(Christ. usage.)</i> Spiritual milk.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானப்பிள்ளை</tam>, <i>s. (Christ. usage.)</i> A god-son or god-daughter.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபோசனம்</tam>, <i>s. (Christ. usage.)</i> Spiritual food.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானபோதகம்</tam>–<tam>ஞானபோதனை</tam>, <i>s.</i> Instruction in the mysteries of religion, spiritual or divine instruction.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானப்பிரகாரம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual nature, manner, mode, &c.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானப்பிராந்தி</tam>, <i>s.</i> Absorption or abstraction of mind in the contemplation and enjoyment of divine things.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானப்பொருள்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A spiritual thing.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானமயம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spirituality.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானமார்க்கம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The sublime and spiritual parts of religion. 2. The course of life according to the highest degree of Saivism–as <tam>ஞானநிலை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானமுத்திரை</tam>, <i>s.</i> A distinguishing mark impressed upon a person to denote his religion.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானமூர்த்தி</tam>, <i>s.</i> God, <tam>கடவுள்</tam>. 2. Sarasvati, <tam>சரசுவதி</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானரத்னம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual gem; <i>i. e.</i> the deity.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானரேகை</tam>, <i>s. [in palmistry.]</i> A line on the fourth finger, indicating the acquisition of knowledge.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானவதி</tam>, <i>s.</i> A wise woman.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானவல்லி</tam>, <i>s.</i> Parvati, <tam>பாரவதி</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானவழி</tam>, <i>s.</i> Spiritual religion, true piety. 2. The course of life according to the fourth degree–as <tam>ஞானமார்க்கம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானவாரி</tam>, <i>s.</i> The sea of spiritual knowledge and enjoyment.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானவான்</tam>–<tam>ஞானவந்தன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> One who has attained a knowledge of the mysteries of religion. 2. A <tam>ஞானி</tam>, or one of the fourth degrees in the Saiva system. <i>(c.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>ஞானவிரல்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The finger next to the little finger.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானவீரர்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The valiant enthusiasts in the higher degrees of religion.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Brahma–as <tam>ஞானி</tam>, <tam>பிரமன்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாகரன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The deity, as the source of wisdom; [<i>ex</i> <tam>ஆகரம்</tam>, mine.]</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாகாசம்</tam>–<tam>ஞானாகாயம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The spiritual vacuum of the <tam>ஞானி</tam> by which he affects to perceive, at once, every thing in the universe.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாசத்தி</tam>, <i>s.</i> One of the three perfections of the deity, knowledge of the actions performed by souls and which causes them to enjoy or suffer the fruit of those actions. 2. One of the five perfections of the deity, that power of god which exists as the five senses.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாசாரம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Religious conduct according to the higher stages, fourth or highest degree; prastice of the sage who has renounced secularities, to whom the pearl and its shell are of equal value; [<i>ex</i> <tam>ஆசாரம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாசாரியன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A spiritual teacher–as <tam>ஞானகுரு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாதிக்கம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The possession of wisdom.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாத்துமா</tam>, <i>s.</i> A wise (holy) soul.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாமிர்ததடாகம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A Roman Catholic work in Tamil containing the doctrines of the Romish church; <i>(lit.)</i> a tank of spiritual nectar.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாயுதம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A spiritual armor or weapon.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானார்த்தம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The true meaning; the spiritual sense; [<i>ex</i> <tam>அர்த்தம்</tam>.]</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானாவரணீயம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The obscuration of wisdom, <tam>ஞானமங்குதல்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானானந்தம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The sublime spiritual enjoyments of religion.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானானந்தன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The deity, full of spiritual delight.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானானுட்டானம்</tam>–<tam>ஞானாநுஷ்டானம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The practice of the <tam>ஞானி</tam>–as <tam>ஞானநிட்டை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானானுபவம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The enjoyment of wisdom.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானானுபானதிரவியம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Sacraments.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானானுபானம்</tam>, <i>s. (Christ. usage.)</i> Means of grace, sacraments; [<i>ex</i> <tam>அனுபானம்</tam>, a vehicle.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானி</tam>, <i>s.</i> A sage, one possessing the knowledge of deity, souls, &c., a man of sublime religious knowledge. <tam>அறிவுள்ளோன்</tam>. 2. A man of the fourth and highest degree in the Saiva system. <tam>நாலாம்பாதத்தோன்</tam>. 3. Brahma of the Triad, <tam>பிரமன்</tam>. 4. Argha of the Jaina sect, <tam>அருகன்</tam>. 5. A gallinaceous fowl, a cock as knowing the hours of the night, <tam>சேவல்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானேந்திரியம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The five organs of sense and perception, as the eye, &c. See <tam>இந்திரியம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானோதயம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The dawn of spiritual wisdom in the soul, when, by the influence of divine grace, the desires for secular objects are subjected, and the soul tends toward union with the deity. 2. A poem containing thirty wise <tam>விருத்தம்</tam> of <tam>அகஸ்தியர்</tam>; [<i>ex</i> <tam>உதயம்</tam>.]</p2> <p2><tam>ஞானோபதேசம்</tam>–<tam>ஞானோபதேயம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Instruction by a guru, or by the deity in human form, in the sublimities, mysteries, &c., of religion. 2. Spiritual instruction in general; [<i>ex</i> <tam>உபதேசம்</tam>.]</p2> <p2><tam>வாசாஞானம்</tam>–<tam>வாய்ஞானம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Speculative knowledge.</p2> <p2><tam>உலகஞானம்</tam>, <i>s. (Christ. usage.)</i> Wisdom of this world.</p2> <p2><tam>மெய்ஞ்ஞானம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> True wisdom; [<i>ex</i> <tam>மெய்</tam>.]</p2> <p2><tam>அஞ்ஞானம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Ignorance, heathenism; [<i>ex</i> <tam>அ</tam> <i>priv.</i>]</p2> <p2><tam>பரமஞானம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Divine wisdom; [<i>ex</i> <tam>பரமம்</tam>.]</p2></p> </blockquote>
		</div>

    <div class="modal-content">
      <div class="modal-header">

        <button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
          <span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>

<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/jquery-3.2.1.min.js"></script>
<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/popper.min.js"></script>
<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/bootstrap.min.js"></script>

<script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
        $(document).keypress(function(event) {
                var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keycode == "116") {
                        var selection = window.getSelection().toString();
			var q_param = $.trim(selection);
			q_param = q_param.replace(/[;]/g, '%3B');
			var q_param = q_param.replace(/\/?#/g,'')
			//console.log(selection)
			//console.log(q_param)
			var q_url = 'tamil/get_transliteration.py?q=' + q_param;
			$.ajax({
				url:q_url,
				dataType: "text"
			}).done(function(data){
				//console.log(data)
				var title_text = selection.replace(/\u00a0\u00a0/g,'\u00a0') 
				title_text = title_text.replace(/\u00a0/g,'<br/>')
				var title = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">Transliteration for: ' + title_text + '</span>';
				var display_data = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">' + data + '</span>';
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').html(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').html(display_data);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			}).fail(function(xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
				console.log(xhr)
				console.log(ajaxOptions)
				console.log(thrownError)
				if (thrownError === 'Request-URI Too Long') {
					var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				}
				else if (thrownError === 'Internal Server Error') {
					var message = "The transliteration code encountered a problem. Please try again.";
				}
				var title = "Error: " + thrownError;
				//var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').text(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').text(message);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			});
                };
        });
    });

</script>
